#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#  International Frogans Address Pattern - IFAP 1.1
#  IFAP Lookup Table
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#
#  Reference: ILT02_Canonical_Mapping
#
#  Description: This IFAP lookup table contains a list of code points in
#  the string character set used in Frogans address strings with, for
#  each code point, the canonical mapping and an indication of whether
#  the code point has the Full_Composition_Exclusion property.  This
#  lookup table is used in the |c2_decompose_compatibility_cp| and
#  |c2_compose| functions defined in Appendix C.2 and in the
#  |c6_decompose_canonical_cp| function defined in Appendix C.6 of the
#  IFAP specification document.
#
#  File name:     ifap11-adopted.spec.ilt02-canonical-mapping.txt
#  File created:  2014-11-07T14:35:17Z
#
#  For additional information on the format of IFAP lookup tables, see
#  Appendix A in the IFAP specification document.
#
#  For additional information on the use of IFAP lookup tables, see
#  Appendix C in the IFAP specification document.
#
#  Properties mentioned in this document are those defined in the
#  Unicode Standard.
#
#  This document is accessible at the following permanent URL:
#  https://www.frogans.org/en/resources/ifap/access.html.
#
#  This document must be used in compliance with the Frogans Technology
#  User Policy, accessible at the following permanent URL:
#  https://www.frogans.org/en/resources/ftup/access.html.
#
#  Copyright (C) 2014 OP3FT.  All rights reserved.
#

#  Third-party source materials used to create this lookup table
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------

#

#    characters and their properties.  For details on the format and
#    contents of this file, see revision 14 of the Unicode Standard
#    Annex #44 at
#    http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr44/tr44-14.html.
#
#  - Copyright and Permission Notice:

#    Distributed under the Terms of Use in
#    http://www.unicode.org/copyright.html.
#

#    obtaining a copy of the Unicode data files and any associated
#    documentation (the "Data Files") or Unicode software and any
#    associated documentation (the "Software") to deal in the Data Files
#    or Software without restriction, including without limitation the
#    rights to use, copy, modify, merge, publish, distribute, and/or
#    sell copies of the Data Files or Software, and to permit persons to
#    whom the Data Files or Software are furnished to do so, provided
#    that (a) the above copyright notice(s) and this permission notice
#    appear with all copies of the Data Files or Software, (b) both the
#    above copyright notice(s) and this permission notice appear in
#    associated documentation, and (c) there is clear notice in each
#    modified Data File or in the Software as well as in the
#    documentation associated with the Data File(s) or Software that the
#    data or software has been modified.
#
#
#  File: HangulSyllableType.txt
#
#  - Location:
#    http://www.unicode.org/Public/7.0.0/ucd/HangulSyllableType.txt
#
#  - Description:
#    HangulSyllableType.txt is a file in the Unicode Character Database
#    of version 7.0.0 of the Unicode Standard.  It lists the values L,
#    V, T, LV, and LVT of the Hangul_Syllable_Type property.  For
#    details on the format and contents of this file, see revision 14 of
#    the Unicode Standard Annex #44 at
#    http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr44/tr44-14.html.
#
#  - Copyright and Permission Notice:
#    See the Copyright and Permission Notice for the UnicodeData.txt
#    file above.
#
#
#  File: DerivedNormalizationProps.txt
#
#  - Location:
#    http://www.unicode.org/Public/7.0.0/ucd/DerivedNormalizationProps.txt
#
#  - Description:
#    DerivedNormalizationProps.txt is a file in the Unicode Character
#    Database of version 7.0.0 of the Unicode Standard.  It lists
#    derived properties used to optimize normalization.  For details on
#    the format and contents of this file, see revision 14 of the
#    Unicode Standard Annex #44 at
#    http://www.unicode.org/reports/tr44/tr44-14.html.
#
#  - Copyright and Permission Notice:
#    See the Copyright and Permission Notice for the UnicodeData.txt
#    file above.
#
#
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#  Other IFAP lookup tables used to create this lookup table
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#
#  ILT01_Character_Set
#
#
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#  Description of the fields in this lookup table
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#
#  Field count: 3
#
#
#  Field 1: CODE_POINT
#
#  - Description:
#    A code point
#
#
#  Field 2: CANONICAL_MAPPING
#
#  - Description:
#    A list of one or more code points separated by the ASCII character
#    ' ' (Space)
#
#
#  Field 3: FULL_COMPOSITION_EXCLUSION
#
#  - Description:
#    A numerical value, either 1 (meaning that the code point has the
#    Full_Composition_Exclusion property) or 0 (meaning that the code
#    point does not have that property)
#
#
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#  Method used to compute the field values in this lookup table
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#
#  The data lines following these comments are created by reading each
#  data line in ILT01_Character_Set.  If the data line contains a code
#  point range, then the process described below is performed for each
#  code point in the range.  If a code point is skipped in the process
#  below, then the process continues with the next code point.
#
#  Each code point is looked up in UnicodeData.txt and the sixth field
#  in UnicodeData.txt is analyzed.
#
#  If the sixth field in UnicodeData.txt is empty, the code point is
#  looked up in HangulSyllableType.txt.
#
#  If the code point is found in HangulSyllableType.txt, it represents a
#  precomposed Hangul syllable and its canonical decomposition mapping
#  is calculated using the canonical mapping process described in the
#  Unicode Standard section 3.12 Conjoining Jamo Behavior (see the
#  Arithmetic decomposition mapping algorithm in the Hangul Syllable
#  Decomposition section).  Then the process continues with the look-up
#  for the code point in the DerivedNormalizationProps.txt file, as
#  described below.
#
#  If the code point is not found in HangulSyllableType.txt, then the
#  code point is skipped.
#
#  If the sixth field in UnicodeData.txt is not empty, it includes one
#  or two properties.  The first is an optional tag between angle
#  brackets corresponding to the Decomposition_Type, and the second is a
#  list of one or more space-separated code points corresponding to the
#  Decomposition_Mapping property.  If a tag is present, the code point
#  is skipped.  Otherwise, the canonical decomposition mapping of the
#  code point corresponds to the list.
#
#  Then a look-up is performed for the code point in the
#  DerivedNormalizationProps.txt file to see if a line exists containing
#  either this code point or a range including this code point, and
#  where the second field in the semi-colon separated list equals the
#  character string 'Full_Composition_Exclusion'.  If such a line
#  exists, the code point is considered to have the
#  Full_Composition_Exclusion property.  Otherwise, the code point is
#  considered not to have that property.
#
#  A data line is added to ILT02_Canonical_Mapping with the values of
#  the three fields CODE_POINT, CANONICAL_MAPPING, and
#  FULL_COMPOSITION_EXCLUSION:
#
#  - The first value contains the code point.
#  - The second value is the list of one or more space-separated code
#    points corresponding to canonical decomposition mapping of that
#    code point.
#  - The third value contains 1 if the code point has the
#    Full_Composition_Exclusion property, or 0 otherwise.
#
#
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#  Generated data lines
#  ---------------------------------------------------------------------
#
CODE_POINT,CANONICAL_MAPPING,FULL_COMPOSITION_EXCLUSION
